# Text Elements
AFusionBaseActor
{
    bool bIsHide; // 已有：view中显隐 和 非视频模式下显隐

    bool bIsVisibleInVideo; // 已有：模型关键帧显隐

    bool bIsVisibileInVideoAnimation; // 0: 隐藏
                                   // 1 : 显示, 可能来自于前、后可见性开关
                                               也可能是正在播放动画
                                               无动画
} ^8QY60Fur

FFusionLayer
{
    bool bIsVisibleInVideo; // 已有： 图层关键帧显隐
} ^tohL2te8

bool AFusionBaseActor::VisiableInLayer()
{
    	bool bCondition = true;
    	auto DecorateManager = ADecorateManager::GetDecorateManagerInstance();
    	if (DecorateManager->IsVideoMode())
    	{
        bCondition = GetVisibleInVideo() && GetVisibileInVideoAnimation();
    	}
    if (UElementList::IsElementListAvailable())
    {
        return UElementList::GetElementListInstance()->FusionActorVisiable(this) && bCondition;
    }
    return !GetHideStatus() && !GetIsDeleted() && bCondition;
}
 ^rE3NMq6U

显隐逻辑 ^hQwWefGR

创建动画：
1.  方案1：需要一个 Creator 负责创建动画，内部实现鼠标选择模型的逻辑；
   方案2：存一个创建动画的内存状态，继承或修改原本的多选tool，复用已有的多选逻辑

2. 监听快捷键 ctrl 和 G，并切换对应的选择逻辑、高亮逻辑

3. 每次模型列表更新，要更新左侧边栏模型列表

4. 将生成的动画插入当前clip的动画列表【只要点template就另起一行，点Animation后的+再选template就加在选中animation的后面】 ^9sI6bfUc

FClipAnimation ^VDERrM4Z

FAnimation ^SfnSYfF7

    FString Id;

    // type
    EAnimationType Type;

    FString Name;

// ------- 时间相关 -------
    // 起始时间
    float StartTime;

   // 时间间隔
    float ModelInterval;

    // 持续时长
    float Duration; 

    // 有效动画范围，(-1, -1) 表示没有裁切过
    FVector2D TimeRange;

    // 运动方式 -- 两个切线构成一个贝塞尔曲线
    // 管理time vs time 的曲线，和view的运动方式一致
    FVector2f MoveInTangent;
    FVector2f MoveOutTangent;

// ------- 其他基础参数 -------

    // 移动距离
    float Distance;

    // 动画前、后模型的可见性
    bool bVisibilityBefore;
    bool bVisibilityAfter;

    // 移动方向 x, y, z
    FVector Direction;

// -------- 效果叠加选项 --------

    // 旋转 绕用户自定义的局部坐标轴旋转
    bool bSelfRotate;
    int Axis;
    float RotationDegrees;
    bool RotationReverse;

    // 弹性缩放
    bool bResilientScaling;

    // 落地反弹
    bool bBounceBack;
    
// -------- 模型列表 ---------
    // 运行时
    TArray<AFusionBaseActor*> ActorList;

    // 序列化
    TArray<FString> ActorIds; ^1Rm4vLD7

// 用于视频插值时，从最高优先级的行开始给模型设置位置，标记已经设置过的模型，避免被后面行覆盖 ^9OpV1DwY

// 要么增删改Animations和动画内部的模型列表时更新，要么插值时更新 ^68KinRWi

// 记录存在于Animations的组模型的所有子模型。用于判断是否可以drive animation 和 模型关键帧 ^UOncOhaa

void FAnimation::DriveAnimation(float Time, TArray<AFusionBaseActor*>& ActorTransSetted)
{
    float AnimeTime = Time - StartTime; // 动画内部的直接
    // 考虑剪切后的有效时间
    if(TimeRange.X != -1 && AnimeTime < TimeRange.X)
    {
        return;	
    }
    if(TimeRange.Y != -1 && AnimeTime > TimeRange.Y)
    {
        return;	
    }
    
    // Transform 插值
    int NumActors = ActorList.Num();
    float SingleActorAnimationPeriod = Duration - ModelInterval * (NumActors - 1);
    for(int i = 0; i < NumActors; ++i)
    {
        float ActorStartTime = i * ModelInterval;
        // 模型没有被高优先级的动画设置过Transform，且当前时间下正在对该模型进行动画插值
        if(IsActorValid(ActorList[i]) &&!ActorTransSetted.Contains(ActorList[i]) && 
            AnimeTime >= ActorStartTime && AnimeTime <= (ActorStartTime + SingleActorAnimationPeriod))
        {
            // 模型在自己的时间区间内，进行时间分布的再映射
            float ActorAnimeScale = FindScaleAtTime(MoveInTangent, MoveOutTangent, (AnimeTime - ActorStartTime)/SingleActorAnimationPeriod);

            // 每个动画内模型的起始Transform 都是进入视频模式的transform
            FTransform ActorTransform;// find from ActorsOutSide

            // 根据动画类型，获取起始状态是ActorTransform，百分比是ActorAnimeScale时的Transform
            CalcTransformAtScale(ActorTransform, ActorAnimeScale);
            ActorList[i]->SetActorTransform(ActorTransform);
            
            RigRail->UpdateGroupActor(ActorList[i]); // 当前选中组更新bounding box

            // 更新标记，该模型已经被动画设置过transform
            ActorTransSetted.Add(ActorList[i]);
        }
    }
} ^3xpDRhNx

Drive Transform ^9Sg3JsHS

// 传入的Scale已经是被运动方式影响了时间分布的Scale，所以函数内部直接取值即可
void FAnimation::CalcTransformAtScale(FTransform& Trans, float Scale)
{    
    auto BounceDecay =[]
     (float omega, float phi, float decay, float Scale)
    {
        return FMath::Exp(-decay * Scale) * FMath::Abs(FMath::Sin(omega * Scale + phi));
    };
    

    auto easeOutBack = [] (float Scale)
    {
        const float c1 = 1.70158
        const float c3 = c1 + 1
        
        // 计算函数值，并将输出映射回0到1的范围
        return 1 + c3 * FMath::Pow(Scale - 1, 3) + c1 * FMath::Pow(Scale - 1, 2)
    };

    switch(Type)
    {
        // change location Animations Algos:
        case EAnimationType::Fall: // 顶部跌落 +Distance -> 0 
        {
            float ZDistance = 0;
            if(bBounceBack)
            {
                ZDistance  = Distance * BounceDecay(PI * 1.5，PI * 0.5，2, Scale);
            }
            else
            {
                ZDistance  = Distance * (1 - Scale);
            }
            Trans.SetLocation(Trans.GetLocation() + FVector(0,0,Z));
            
        }
        break;
        case EAnimationType::Rise // 顶部飞起 0 -> +Distance 
        {
            float ZDistance = Distance * scale;
            Trans.SetLocation(Trans.GetLocation() + FVector(0,0, ZDistance));
            break;
        }
        case EAnimationType::Emerge // 地面升起 -Distance -> 0
        {
            float ZDistance = 0;
            if(bBounceBack)
            {
                ZDistance  = (-Distance) * easeOutBack(Scale);
            }
            else
            {
                ZDistance  = -Distance * Scale;
            }
            Trans.SetLocation(Trans.GetLocation() + FVector(0,0,Z));
            break;
        }
        // ...
        
        // change Scale3D
        case EAnimationType::ScaleUp:
        {
            float Scale3DScale = Scale;
            if(bResilientScaling)
            {
                Scale3DScale  = easeOutBack(Scale);
            }
            Trans.SetScale3D(Trans.GetScale3D() * Scale3DScale);

            break;
        }
        case EAnimationType::ScaleDown:
        {
            float Scale3DScale = 1 - Scale;
            if(bResilientScaling)
            {
                Scale3DScale  = easeOutBack(1 - Scale);
            }
            Trans.SetScale3D(Trans.GetScale3D() * Scale3DScale);

            break;
        }
        default:
            break;
    }
    
    if(bSelfRotate) // +- RotationDegrees -> 0
    {
        float Rotate = (RotationReverse ? -1 : 1) * RotationDegrees * (1 - Scale);
        FVector LocalRoateVec = FVector::ZeroVector;
        switch(Axis)
        {
        case 0:
            LocalRoateVec .X = Rotate;
            break;
        case 1:
            LocalRoateVec .Y = Rotate;
            break;
        case 2:
            LocalRoateVec .Z = Rotate;
            break;
        }
        FRotator WorldRotation = Trans.GetRotation();
        FVector WorldRotationVec = WorldRotation.RotateVector(LocalRoateVec);
        WorldRotation = WorldRotationVec.Rotation();
        Trans.SetRotation(WorldRotation);
    
    }

} ^8Mgn5P9O

其中A是初始高度，omega是振动的频率，phi是初始相位，decay是衰减系数 ^sVcuNveB

右侧边栏操作命令：
添加、删除、上一个、下一个、预览动画、暂停动画、...

右侧边栏动画API参数列表 ^PJnTyl83

一. 视频模块增加状态PreviewAnimation ^u3kF1HvJ

二. 增加两个接口PreviewAnimationStart, PreviewAnimationStop：

    1. PreviewAnimationStart 预览动画：
        1. 接收要预览的 Animtion 的 Id ，并存储到 FAnimationManager::PreviewAniId
        2. RigRail 把状态设置到 PreviewAnimation
        3. 初始化预览起始状态：FAnimationManager::PreviewTime = 0
        4. 调用一次AnimationManager.PreviewAnimation(0) 把模型状态设置到起始状态
    
    2. PreviewAnimationStop 暂停预览：
        RigRail 把状态设置回Normal，FAnimationManager::PreviewTime = 0 ^UmAHmukv

三. RigRail::tick 时如果发现当前是预览动画的状态，会触发预览并return ^JtHaXERp

四. 预览动画时，如果以任何形式改变了Status会停止预览 ^ChJUf0SG

数据结构 ^YBhtc6X2

预览动画 ^gOWM3da1

轨迹展示Actor ^76KFBAnO

在每个模型在所属动画，自己开始运动的时候要其实也要打一个显示关键帧，
但是又为了找到模型第一个生效的向前可见性关键帧，又要记录在同一时刻打上向前可见性的关键帧
所以干脆，ActorVisibilityFrames不要管模型开始运动的可见性关键帧了，
只记录最早的 向前可见性关键帧 和每个模型在每个动画结束时的向后可见性关键帧 ^qNFKspn9

			"text": "void FAnimation::DriveAnimation(float Time, TArray<AFusionBaseActor*>& ActorTransSetted)\n{\n    float AnimeTime = Time - StartTime; // 动画内部的直接\n    // 考虑剪切后的有效时间\n    if(TimeRange.X != -1 && AnimeTime < TimeRange.X)\n    {\n        return;\t\n    }\n    if(TimeRange.Y != -1 && AnimeTime > TimeRange.Y)\n    {\n        return;\t\n    }\n    \n    // Transform 插值\n    int NumActors = ActorList.Num();\n    float SingleActorAnimationPeriod = Duration - ModelInterval * (NumActors - 1);\n    for(int i = 0; i < NumActors; ++i)\n    {\n        float ActorStartTime = i * ModelInterval;\n        // 模型没有被高优先级的动画设置过Transform，且当前时间下正在对该模型进行动画插值\n        if(IsActorValid(ActorList[i]) &&!ActorTransSetted.Contains(ActorList[i]) && \n            AnimeTime >= ActorStartTime && AnimeTime <= (ActorStartTime + SingleActorAnimationPeriod))\n        {\n            // 模型在自己的时间区间内，进行时间分布的再映射\n            float ActorAnimeScale = FindScaleAtTime(MoveInTangent, MoveOutTangent, (AnimeTime - ActorStartTime)/SingleActorAnimationPeriod);\n\n            // 每个动画内模型的起始Transform 都是进入视频模式的transform\n            FTransform ActorTransform;// find from ActorsOutSide\n\n            // 根据动画类型，获取起始状态是ActorTransform，百分比是ActorAnimeScale时的Transform\n            CalcTransformAtScale(ActorTransform, ActorAnimeScale);\n            ActorList[i]->SetActorTransform(ActorTransform);\n            \n            RigRail->UpdateGroupActor(ActorList[i]); // 当前选中组更新bounding box\n\n            // 更新标记，该模型已经被动画设置过transform\n            ActorTransSetted.Add(ActorList[i]);\n        }\n    }\n}",
			"rawText": "void FAnimation::DriveAnimation(float Time, TArray<AFusionBaseActor*>& ActorTransSetted)\n{\n    float AnimeTime = Time - StartTime; // 动画内部的直接\n    // 考虑剪切后的有效时间\n    if(TimeRange.X != -1 && AnimeTime < TimeRange.X)\n    {\n        return;\t\n    }\n    if(TimeRange.Y != -1 && AnimeTime > TimeRange.Y)\n    {\n        return;\t\n    }\n    \n    // Transform 插值\n    int NumActors = ActorList.Num();\n    float SingleActorAnimationPeriod = Duration - ModelInterval * (NumActors - 1);\n    for(int i = 0; i < NumActors; ++i)\n    {\n        float ActorStartTime = i * ModelInterval;\n        // 模型没有被高优先级的动画设置过Transform，且当前时间下正在对该模型进行动画插值\n        if(IsActorValid(ActorList[i]) &&!ActorTransSetted.Contains(ActorList[i]) && \n            AnimeTime >= ActorStartTime && AnimeTime <= (ActorStartTime + SingleActorAnimationPeriod))\n        {\n            // 模型在自己的时间区间内，进行时间分布的再映射\n            float ActorAnimeScale = FindScaleAtTime(MoveInTangent, MoveOutTangent, (AnimeTime - ActorStartTime)/SingleActorAnimationPeriod);\n\n            // 每个动画内模型的起始Transform 都是进入视频模式的transform\n            FTransform ActorTransform;// find from ActorsOutSide\n\n            // 根据动画类型，获取起始状态是ActorTransform，百分比是ActorAnimeScale时的Transform\n            CalcTransformAtScale(ActorTransform, ActorAnimeScale);\n            ActorList[i]->SetActorTransform(ActorTransform);\n            \n            RigRail->UpdateGroupActor(ActorList[i]); // 当前选中组更新bounding box\n\n            // 更新标记，该模型已经被动画设置过transform\n            ActorTransSetted.Add(ActorList[i]);\n        }\n    }\n}",

			"text": "// 传入的Scale已经是被运动方式影响了时间分布的Scale，所以函数内部直接取值即可\nvoid FAnimation::CalcTransformAtScale(FTransform& Trans, float Scale)\n{    \n    auto BounceDecay =[]\n     (float omega, float phi, float decay, float Scale)\n    {\n        return FMath::Exp(-decay * Scale) * FMath::Abs(FMath::Sin(omega * Scale + phi));\n    };\n    \n\n    auto easeOutBack = [] (float Scale)\n    {\n        const float c1 = 1.70158\n        const float c3 = c1 + 1\n        \n        // 计算函数值，并将输出映射回0到1的范围\n        return 1 + c3 * FMath::Pow(Scale - 1, 3) + c1 * FMath::Pow(Scale - 1, 2)\n    };\n\n    switch(Type)\n    {\n        // change location Animations Algos:\n        case EAnimationType::Fall: // 顶部跌落 +Distance -> 0 \n        {\n            float ZDistance = 0;\n            if(bBounceBack)\n            {\n                ZDistance  = Distance * BounceDecay(PI * 1.5，PI * 0.5，2, Scale);\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                ZDistance  = Distance * (1 - Scale);\n            }\n            Trans.SetLocation(Trans.GetLocation() + FVector(0,0,Z));\n            \n        }\n        break;\n        case EAnimationType::Rise // 顶部飞起 0 -> +Distance \n        {\n            float ZDistance = Distance * scale;\n            Trans.SetLocation(Trans.GetLocation() + FVector(0,0, ZDistance));\n            break;\n        }\n        case EAnimationType::Emerge // 地面升起 -Distance -> 0\n        {\n            float ZDistance = 0;\n            if(bBounceBack)\n            {\n                ZDistance  = (-Distance) * easeOutBack(Scale);\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                ZDistance  = -Distance * Scale;\n            }\n            Trans.SetLocation(Trans.GetLocation() + FVector(0,0,Z));\n            break;\n        }\n        // ...\n        \n        // change Scale3D\n        case EAnimationType::ScaleUp:\n        {\n            float Scale3DScale = Scale;\n            if(bResilientScaling)\n            {\n                Scale3DScale  = easeOutBack(Scale);\n            }\n            Trans.SetScale3D(Trans.GetScale3D() * Scale3DScale);\n\n            break;\n        }\n        case EAnimationType::ScaleDown:\n        {\n            float Scale3DScale = 1 - Scale;\n            if(bResilientScaling)\n            {\n                Scale3DScale  = easeOutBack(1 - Scale);\n            }\n            Trans.SetScale3D(Trans.GetScale3D() * Scale3DScale);\n\n            break;\n        }\n        default:\n            break;\n    }\n    \n    if(bSelfRotate) // +- RotationDegrees -> 0\n    {\n        float Rotate = (RotationReverse ? -1 : 1) * RotationDegrees * (1 - Scale);\n        FVector LocalRoateVec = FVector::ZeroVector;\n        switch(Axis)\n        {\n        case 0:\n            LocalRoateVec .X = Rotate;\n            break;\n        case 1:\n            LocalRoateVec .Y = Rotate;\n            break;\n        case 2:\n            LocalRoateVec .Z = Rotate;\n            break;\n        }\n        FRotator WorldRotation = Trans.GetRotation();\n        FVector WorldRotationVec = WorldRotation.RotateVector(LocalRoateVec);\n        WorldRotation = WorldRotationVec.Rotation();\n        Trans.SetRotation(WorldRotation);\n    \n    }\n\n}",
